      <p>
       This is a
       <b>
        list of solar eclipses in the 8th century
       </b>
       . During the period 701 to 800 there were 233
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">
        solar eclipses
       </a>
       of which 77 were partial, 88 were annular (two
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse#Terminology" title="Solar eclipse">
        non-central
       </a>
       ), 66 were total, and 2 were hybrids. The greatest number of eclipses in one year was five, in 734.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Dates are given using the
       <a href="/wiki/Julian_calendar" title="Julian calendar">
        Julian calendar
       </a>
       .
      </p>

            </sup>
           </a>

             <i>

             </i>
            </sup>
           </a>
          </span>

            </th>
            <td class="navbox-list navbox-even" style="text-align:left;border-left-width:2px;border-left-style:solid;width:100%;padding:0px">
             <div style="padding:0em 0.25em">
